The joke is that the kanji for “plum” (梅), which also reads as “ka” is used in his family name, and his given name was turned into “mazuo,” which is a pun on “mazui” (まずい), i.e. something that sucks."},"originalLanguage":"ja","publicationDemographic":"seinen","contentRating":"safe","tags":[{"id":"0234a31e-a729-4e28-9d6a-3f87c4966b9e","name":{"en":"Oneshot"}},{"id":"4d32cc48-9f00-4cca-9b5a-a839f0764984","name":{"en":"Comedy"}},{"id":"cdad7e68-1419-41dd-bdce-27753074a640","name":{"en":"Horror"}}]}
